  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_07ac024e-636e-4398-b8ce-464e11f00e3a'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer1778816096491067870"><b>The first book in a brand new series from bestselling author Sarah Robinson, Logan's Story is a glimpse into the famous rockstars past and how he achieved his fame. Before the lights, stage, and music, Logan Clay struggles to figure out who he can trust and whether or not love comes with guitar strings attached. </b><br/> <br/>Logan Clay has the talent, and he's put in the time. <br/>All he </span>
  <span id="freeText1778816096491067870" style="display:none"><b>The first book in a brand new series from bestselling author Sarah Robinson, Logan's Story is a glimpse into the famous rockstars past and how he achieved his fame. Before the lights, stage, and music, Logan Clay struggles to figure out who he can trust and whether or not love comes with guitar strings attached. </b><br /> <br />Logan Clay has the talent, and he's put in the time. <br />All he needs is that one big break,<br />just one chance to prove he has what it takes to be a rockstar. <br />But his musical dreams are further away than ever...<br /><br />And then she walks in to his life,<br />offering him everything he's ever wanted - fame, fortune, and music. <br />There's no question that he's going to take the chance,<br />or that he wants to take her at the same time.<br /><br />But everything is not what it seems.<br />Will it be too late when he realizes his one big break <br />was actually a deal with the devil in a short skirt and neon colored hair?<br /><br /> <br /><i>DISCLAIMER: This book was originally published in June 2014 with the title "Logan's Story: A Sand &amp; Clay Prequel" by Sarah Robinson. Since then it has been re-edited, a few short scenes here and there added in, and given a new title and a new cover in order to improve the novel. This is the final product of that revision process so there have been a lot of changes, but the story itself is relatively the same. This novel is meant for 18+ years old.</i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=music">music</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1149437166" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1232757655855909707"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/sandandclayFeatIMG_zps71f3370b.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420154914i/13183139._SX540_.png' alt=' photo sandandclayFeatIMG_zps71f3370b.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Logan’s Story is #0.5 in the Sand Clay series by Sarah Robinson. <br/><br/>Logan Clay is very close to his parents. His mother is in a wheel chair and his father cares for her full time so the responsibility of paying the bills falls on Logan’s shoulders. It’s a huge responsibility but one he easily accepts. There is one thing, though, that Logan might love more than even his family. His music. At a young age he showed a natural ability with the guitar and it soon became his life. Now as an adult, he’</span>
  <span id="freeText1232757655855909707" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/sandandclayFeatIMG_zps71f3370b.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420154914i/13183139._SX540_.png" alt=" photo sandandclayFeatIMG_zps71f3370b.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Logan’s Story is #0.5 in the Sand Clay series by Sarah Robinson. <br><br>Logan Clay is very close to his parents. His mother is in a wheel chair and his father cares for her full time so the responsibility of paying the bills falls on Logan’s shoulders. It’s a huge responsibility but one he easily accepts. There is one thing, though, that Logan might love more than even his family. His music. At a young age he showed a natural ability with the guitar and it soon became his life. Now as an adult, he’s trying to make it into a career. He and his band have been playing small time bars and have a following but it doesn’t pay the bills. But finally, his big break might be within his grasp. A famous scout is coming from New York to hear them play. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/399bff496169d0402be56ad8_640_zpsdbd1e67f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420154914i/13183140._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 399bff496169d0402be56ad8_640_zpsdbd1e67f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Tonight was the night. This was his chance.”</i>
</b><br><br>Logan doesn’t have time for women. Between his regular job, his gigs, and spending time with his parents, he can barely fit in any time for sleep. But the same night the scout was supposed to show up, he meets Gina Vile in the bar, not realizing she was the daughter of the scout, Garrett Vile. The attraction is mutually instant. And the gig was one of the best of his life. Is it possible that in one night, everything in his life could change and that his hopes of the life he has dreamed of his entire life might actually come true?<br><br><b>
  <i>“Stole my heart just to throw it away,<br>No explanation for the games you play.<br>Am I just a Friday night to you,<br>Or are we going to see this through?”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/music_zps396c0a59.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384812890i/6982513.jpg" alt=" photo music_zps396c0a59.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As always, though, dreams come at a cost and it is a price Logan has to decide if he is willing to pay. His mother’s health takes a turn for the worse further complicating things. And what about Gina? Are her motivations pure or is he just a rung on the ladder to her own success in the business? <br><br>This was a perfect introduction to Logan’s life. He is a simple man, hugely talented, that just wants to be recognized for his music. And he wants to be able to provide the care for his mother that she deserves. I’ll keep my opinions to myself regarding Gina and let you decide what you think. I can’t wait to continue on to see what is in store next for Logan Clay! <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/Sand-Clay-Series-3-Books-Transparent-Back_zps5266cfc5.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420154914i/13183141._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Sand-Clay-Series-3-Books-Transparent-Back_zps5266cfc5.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer930245301" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9332875163969695848">I really enjoyed beta reading this story for the author. I think this is my new favorite book of hers. This is the prequel to Sand and Clay, and it introduces us to Logan before he becomes a famous rock star, back when he was playing in bars with his band. This story has so much depth and challenging events, I was surprised that it could all fit in a novella. But it works so well, I was gripped by the story, and when I got to the end, I yelled no!<br/>Logan has played guitar his whole life. Now, he f</span>
  <span id="freeText9332875163969695848" style="display:none">I really enjoyed beta reading this story for the author. I think this is my new favorite book of hers. This is the prequel to Sand and Clay, and it introduces us to Logan before he becomes a famous rock star, back when he was playing in bars with his band. This story has so much depth and challenging events, I was surprised that it could all fit in a novella. But it works so well, I was gripped by the story, and when I got to the end, I yelled no!<br />Logan has played guitar his whole life. Now, he finds himself playing gigs at the bar and working 12 hour days in a warehouse to help pay his mother's medical bills, as well as keep a roof over all their heads so his father can take care of his mom, since the accident had made it impossible for her to take care of herself. He loves his family, and he has no regrets. But what happens when a big scout is going to be at their show? What will the guys do? And when bad things happen, what is the right thing to do?<br />This story has so many surprises and twists, it sure feels bigger than a novella, but you can read it in one sitting. And that's a good thing, because I could not rest until I got to the end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9332875163969695848" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

I love Logan Clay. <br/>This story is about Logan Clay before he was a Rockstar. There was so much going on in this story and I did not want to put It down. He would sing at clubs with his band and he would work another job early in the mornings. He hardly got any s</span>
  <span id="freeText7670890214932866551" style="display:none">I was very happy to be asked to be beta reader for this story. This was an amazing story and I love it so much. I love Logan Clay. <br />This story is about Logan Clay before he was a Rockstar. There was so much going on in this story and I did not want to put It down. It had so much emotion in it that I cried a lot. Logan Clay is an amazing man who worked to jobs to help his family pay bills. He would sing at clubs with his band and he would work another job early in the mornings. He hardly got any sleep but he did it for his family. Gina Vile is pretty amazing in this story. I didn't expect everything that happened in this novella to happen. This story explains a lot of what happened with Logan,his family and friends before he became famous. He worked very hard for what he got. He deserved his fame. It also explains why he didn't want to leave Gina in Sand &amp; Clay. It helped me to understand Logan and Gina's relationship a lot. I have found my new favorite book. I really love me some Logan Clay he is so amazing. <br />Everyone should read this book especially if you love a book about Rockstars. Logan Clay is my new Rockstar Book Boyfriend. I love the song in this book it is awesome. I think it was one of my favorite things in the book. This book is a 5 star read for sure. Sarah Robinson is an amazing author and I love all of her books. She is one of those authors I will One Click without even reading about the book first. I really loved this book and I really love this author and I think everyone should read all of her books because she is amazing. Everything in this book was perfect. Which everything in all of her books are always perfect. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16596855676713505125">I read this book first in the Sand & Clay Forbidden Rockstar series. For some really I like reading the prequel first just so I can understand why a character is the way that they are. I am so so happy that I did because it gave a better understanding of Logan Clay and Gina Vile. <br/><br/>In this novella we get tons of information about Logan and his past and why he is where he is in Sand & Clay.   <span id="freeText16596855676713505125" style="display:none">I read this book first in the Sand &amp; Clay Forbidden Rockstar series. For some really I like reading the prequel first just so I can understand why a character is the way that they are. I am so so happy that I did because it gave a better understanding of Logan Clay and Gina Vile. <br /><br />In this novella we get tons of information about Logan and his past and why he is where he is in Sand &amp; Clay. I was able to connect with him better because he got to see who he was before his fame and recognition. He is loyal and has so much responsibility to his family. I also liked his friends that stuck with him during his hard times. His dad is pretty awesome as well as his mom, who both were so proud of their son. In this book you can feel the struggles that Logan is going through to provide for his family all the while trying make it so he can support his family better. I liked the chemistry between him and Gina in this novella BEFORE the fame and success got mixed in with their personal relationship. <br /><br />This book is a must read in order to better connect and understand Logan in Sand &amp; Clay...which I am going to review now!</span>

He couldn't even imagine how his life would be growing up. But with the help of his ever patient father and circle of friends, Logan became the hardworking, passionate, adored man he is today. <br/><br/>Reading about his past and the events that unfolded before rising to his rockstar status was a good way of introducing Logan, the man of the hour. His fascination with</span>
  <span id="freeText18117019555587905717" style="display:none">Through the eyes of a child, seeing his father tear up after learning that his mother could no longer use or feel her legs was devastating. He couldn't even imagine how his life would be growing up. But with the help of his ever patient father and circle of friends, Logan became the hardworking, passionate, adored man he is today. <br /><br />Reading about his past and the events that unfolded before rising to his rockstar status was a good way of introducing Logan, the man of the hour. His fascination with music, his instant attraction to Gina, his decision whether to stay in a band with his so-called brothers or live his dream, it was all here.<br /><br />I actually read this book 2 days before Christmas Day and I liked it. I liked how Logan started from scratch and made it through wise decisions. I don't like Gina, however.. I just don't like the vibes I get from her. Maybe it's just me.. I don't know... What I do know is, I am intrigued by Caroline Sanders and I can't wait to read Her Forbidden Rockstar!</span>

<div id="review_973601522" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/973601522" />
    <a title="Wendy Ward" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14229252-wendy-ward"><img alt="Wendy Ward" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1351975712p2/14229252.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/973601522?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy Ward" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy Ward" href="/user/show/14229252-wendy-ward">Wendy Ward</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer973601522" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9406178265513423876">Logan is the lead singer of a band offered a shot at getting a contract. The only problem is that the company wants only Logan. Gina is a girl Logan met at the bar, whose father just happens to be the guy that offers Logan a shot with his company. While in New York Logan confesses his love for Gina, but turns tail and runs back home when he finds out that Gina wasn’t exactly forthright in who she was when they met. Will Logan’s Story have a happy ending? <br/>Logan is the epitome of a good guy. He’s </span>
  <span id="freeText9406178265513423876" style="display:none">Logan is the lead singer of a band offered a shot at getting a contract. The only problem is that the company wants only Logan. Gina is a girl Logan met at the bar, whose father just happens to be the guy that offers Logan a shot with his company. While in New York Logan confesses his love for Gina, but turns tail and runs back home when he finds out that Gina wasn’t exactly forthright in who she was when they met. Will Logan’s Story have a happy ending? <br />Logan is the epitome of a good guy. He’s a budding rock star, a good son, and head over heels in love with his girl, Gina. Gina, although not exactly truthful about herself in the beginning of the story turns out to have a genuinely good heart, and so in love with Logan that she becomes the saving grace for someone he loves. The two of them seem perfect for one another and destined for happiness, but with this only being the beginning of their story it may be a longer road to get there. <br />Sarah Robinson is a gifted writer. This story is filled with emotion and complexity. Both her cast of main characters and supporting characters (Dylan, Rock, mom, dad, etc.) are well written and weave such a story that several of them could even have a novel of their own. They are that interesting. Logan’s Story is the prequel for Sand and Clay, which is already available for purchase, so you don’t have to obsessively wait to find out if Logan and Gina’s relationship evolves or implodes. I’m off to start on it now.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9406178265513423876" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText6620765705303010124" style="display:none">This story is full of emotions and loyalty. I fell in love with Logan Clay, he is a tough Irish Man with a very good heart. He has sacrificed a part of himself to be the financial support for his parents. Logan and his band play at small gigs at night and then he works the graveyard shift at a warehouse. Logan is totally dedicated. Music is Logan’s fuel. He feels through his music. He lives through his music. When he meets Gina Vile, she stirs up his feelings; feelings he hadn't felt in a very long time. When Logan is discovered by a Scout, he is ecstatic, but they want him alone and not his band mates. What will he do? Loyalties will be tested. Will he have a chance at fame? This story grasped me and tugged at my heart. I was pulled in and felt Logan’s struggle. I completely loved this story from beginning to end. The ending surprised me a bit, but I can totally see this happening. </span>

  <span id="freeText13032962894972847002" style="display:none">This novella starts off with learning about Logan Clay before he becomes a famous rock star. He is such a caring person and works two jobs to help his family pay the bills while his dad stays at home to care for his mother after her accident. He plays in a band with three of his closest friends in bars. He loves to play and sing music. He meets Gina, who he really connects with since he never really has time for a relationship, this is all new for him. A scout comes to hear his band play to see if he wants to sign them in a record deal but the deal the scout offers isn't what Logan was thinking for him and his band. Will he make the right decision for him or for his band. There is a lot of twists and things that take place in this book that it keeps you wanting to read to see what happens. Can't wait to read Sand and Clay next.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1130417546" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16909953537327773733"><strong>Logan's Story</strong><br/><br/>The story of a struggling singer and guitarist and how he got his start. <br/>Logan Clay is a true mommas boy with a high respect for his family and responsibilities. He works 3rd shift at a factory to help pay the families bills and pursues his dream with his band playing clubs for tips and to be recognized. <br/>Logan's luck changes when he meets Gina and her father and is offered a recording contract. One drawback the contract is only for him not the rest of the band.<br/>Logan has to decide wh</span>
  <span id="freeText16909953537327773733" style="display:none"><strong>Logan's Story</strong><br /><br />The story of a struggling singer and guitarist and how he got his start. <br />Logan Clay is a true mommas boy with a high respect for his family and responsibilities. He works 3rd shift at a factory to help pay the families bills and pursues his dream with his band playing clubs for tips and to be recognized. <br />Logan's luck changes when he meets Gina and her father and is offered a recording contract. One drawback the contract is only for him not the rest of the band.<br />Logan has to decide what is best for himself and his family in order to achieve his dreams.<br />Great novella by Sarah Robinson. <span id="freeTextContainer7708749321211374798">**I was given this eBook from the author for an honest review**<br/><br/>This is the prequel to Sand & Clay series. It introduces us to Logan Clay, a young man that works a 12 hour shift that starts at three AM in a warehouse. When Logan isn't working at the warehouse, he is playing at some of the local bars in the area with his band which contains three of his best friends. He's working to help his parents out. He doesn't have to but he does it because he loves them and wants whats best. This book was wo</span>
  <span id="freeText7708749321211374798" style="display:none">**I was given this eBook from the author for an honest review**<br /><br />This is the prequel to Sand &amp; Clay series. It introduces us to Logan Clay, a young man that works a 12 hour shift that starts at three AM in a warehouse. When Logan isn't working at the warehouse, he is playing at some of the local bars in the area with his band which contains three of his best friends. He's working to help his parents out. He doesn't have to but he does it because he loves them and wants whats best. This book was wonderful in so many ways. There was some ups and downs between all the characters but that's what makes a book good! I seriously couldn't stop reading this when I started it! Definitely a GREAT read!!!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('R10IzgtG0PbXYzIkknj34tUVZOAAi5aIGD9kGdoeO+/kqiVV0QUHYj0GP89UT7iaLaEbx4WpnPY+zBdMBXUrZg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }
